## Idea

A **natural isomorphism** `γ` from [map](category-theory.maps-categories.md)
`F : C → D` to `G : C → D` is a
[natural transformation](category-theory.natural-transformations-maps-categories.md)
from `F` to `G` such that the morphism `γ F : hom (F x) (G x)` is an
[isomorphism](category-theory.isomorphisms-in-categories.md), for every object
`x` in `C`.

## Definition

### Natural isomorphisms in a category

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4611" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4618" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4618" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="4622" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4623" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4623" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="4627" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4627" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="4631" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4631" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="4635" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4635" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="4639" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4641" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4646" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="4650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4651" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4651" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="4654" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4656" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="4666" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4623" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="4670" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4627" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="4673" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Examples

### The identity natural isomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8722" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8729" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8729" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="8733" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8734" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8734" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="8738" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8738" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="8742" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8742" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="8746" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8746" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="8750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8752" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8757" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Equalities induce natural isomorphisms

An equality between maps `F` and `G` gives rise to a natural isomorphism between
them. This is because, by the J-rule, it is enough to construct a natural
isomorphism given `refl : F ＝ F`, from `F` to itself. We take the identity
natural transformation as such an isomorphism.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="natural-isomorphism-map-eq-Categoryᵉ"></a><a id="9430" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9430" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-map-eq-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9467" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9471" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9472" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9472" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="9476" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9476" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="9480" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9480" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="9484" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9484" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="9488" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9490" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9495" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9500" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9500" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9503" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9505" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9515" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9472" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="9519" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9476" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="9522" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9527" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9527" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9530" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9532" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9542" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9480" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="9546" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9484" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="9549" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9553" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9554" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9554" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9557" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9557" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="9560" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9562" href="category-theory.maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#785" class="Function">map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9576" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9500" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9579" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9527" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="9581" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9583" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9587" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9554" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9590" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="9593" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9557" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="9596" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9598" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4745" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9632" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9500" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9635" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9527" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9638" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9554" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9641" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9557" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a>
<a id="9644" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9430" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-map-eq-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9681" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9681" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9684" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9684" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9687" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9687" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9690" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="9691" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9687" class="DottedPattern Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9694" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">reflᵉ</a> <a id="9700" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="9704" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8824" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="9741" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9681" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9744" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9684" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9747" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9687" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a>
</pre>
## Propositions

### Being a natural isomorphism is a proposition

That a natural transformation is a natural isomorphism is a proposition. This
follows from the fact that being an isomorphism is a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9975" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9982" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9982" class="Module">_</a>

### Equality of natural isomorphisms is equality of their underlying natural transformations

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10911" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10918" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10918" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="11738" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5164" class="Function">natural-transformation-map-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="11799" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="11802" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="11805" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="11808" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="11811" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11593" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="11813" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11815" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="11821" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11590" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="11824" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="11827" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11593" class="Bound">gᵉ</a>
  <a id="11832" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11516" class="Function">eq-eq-natural-transformation-map-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="11899" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11899" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="11902" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11902" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="11905" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="11911" href="foundation-core.subtypes%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4286" class="Function">eq-type-subtypeᵉ</a> <a id="11928" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11929" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10481" class="Function">is-natural-isomorphism-map-prop-hom-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="11975" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="11978" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="11981" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="11984" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="11986" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11991" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11991" class="Function">eq-htpy-hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12044" class="Symbol">:</a>
        <a id="12054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12055" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12055" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="12058" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12058" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="12061" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12063" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4745" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12097" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12100" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12103" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12106" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="12108" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12110" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="12116" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12118" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5520" class="Function">hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12163" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12166" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12169" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12172" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="12175" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12055" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="12178" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a>
      <a id="12187" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5520" class="Function">hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12232" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12235" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12238" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12241" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="12244" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12058" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="12246" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12248" class="Symbol">→</a>

  <a id="12265" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11991" class="Function">eq-htpy-hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12318" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="12324" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12343" class="Function">eq-htpy-hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Precategoryᵉ</a>
      <a id="12386" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12388" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12410" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10951" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="12412" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="12420" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12422" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="12444" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10978" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="12446" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="12454" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12456" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11005" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="12458" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="12466" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12468" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11008" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="12470" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The type of natural isomorphisms form a set

The type of natural isomorphisms between maps `F` and `G` is a
[subtype](foundation-core.subtypes.md) of the [set](foundation-core.sets.md)
`natural-transformation F G` since being an isomorphism is a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="12749" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="12756" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12756" class="Module">_</a>

### Inverses of natural isomorphisms are natural isomorphisms

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13519" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13526" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13526" class="Module">_</a>

### Natural isomorphisms are closed under composition

<pre class="Agda"><a id="18855" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18862" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18862" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="23260" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23262" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23284" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22798" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="23286" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23294" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23296" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23318" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22825" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="23320" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23328" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23330" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22852" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="23332" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23340" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23342" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22855" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="23344" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23361" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23361" class="Function">right-unit-law-comp-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23415" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="23421" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20962" class="Function">comp-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23460" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22798" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="23463" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22825" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="23466" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22852" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="23469" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22852" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="23472" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22855" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="23475" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22884" class="Bound">fᵉ</a>
      <a id="23484" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23486" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8824" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23523" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22798" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="23526" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22825" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="23529" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22852" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="23531" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23533" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a>
    <a id="23540" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22884" class="Bound">fᵉ</a>

      <a id="23668" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23670" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23692" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22798" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="23694" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23702" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23704" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2419" class="Function">precategory-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="23726" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22825" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="23728" class="Symbol">)</a>

#### Composition of natural isomorphisms is associative

#### Composition of natural isomorphisms satisfies inverse laws

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24815" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24822" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24822" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="24826" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24827" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24827" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="24831" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24831" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="24835" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24835" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="24839" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24839" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="24843" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24845" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="24850" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="24854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24855" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24855" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="24858" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24860" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="24870" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24827" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="24874" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24831" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="24877" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24882" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24882" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="24885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24887" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="24897" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24835" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="24901" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24839" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="24904" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="25932" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25934" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24909" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="25936" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="25944" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25946" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24912" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="25948" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="25956" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25958" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24941" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="25960" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### When the type of natural transformations is a proposition, The type of natural isomorphisms is a proposition

The type of natural isomorphisms between maps `F` and `G` is a subtype of
`natural-transformation F G`, so when this type is a proposition, then the type
of natural isomorphisms from `F` to `G` form a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="26304" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="26311" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26311" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="26315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26316" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26316" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="26320" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26320" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="26324" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26324" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="26328" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26328" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="26332" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26334" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="26339" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="26343" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26344" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26344" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="26347" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26349" href="category-theory.categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Function">Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="26359" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26316" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="26363" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26320" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="26366" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="26429" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="26438" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-categories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26438" class="Function">is-prop-natural-isomorphism-map-Categoryᵉ</a> <a id="26480" class="Symbol">:</a>

</pre>
### Functoriality of `natural-isomorphism-map-eq`
